event = {

}

}

owned = { province = 1158 data = MON }
owned = { province = 1147 data = MON }
control = { province = 1162 data = RUS }
control = { province = 1161 data = RUS }
}


name = "The Trans-Siberian Crisis"
desc = "Horrible news!  A train full of Russian citizens has been massacred by bandits on the Mongolian section of the Trans-Siberian railroad! Our people are shocked by this act of barbarism and demand an immediate response from the government. This could be an opportunity for us to reassert control over the Far Eastern sections of the railroad but we must tread carefully. Baron Ungern von Sternberg, Supreme Khan of All Mongols, is unhinged and may not take kindly to interference."
picture = "traindestroyed"

offset = 15
